"extremities, dressing. this class includes one or more of 7 standard placement interventions or procedures on component parts of the extremities: dressing.  these placement interventions or procedures are listed in the world health organizations international statistical classification of diseases and related health problems or icd-10 pcs under code 2w.. dressing of left finger using bandage. this classification denotes the group of activities that yields a placement intervention or procedure to dressing of left finger using bandage.this placement intervention or procedure is listed in the world health organizations international statistical classification of diseases and related health problems or icd-10 as code 2w2kx4z.
